# CHANGELOG

All notable changes to Aisha CRM will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).

---

## [Unreleased]

### Fixed

- **Opportunity records with stage="Won"/"Lost" don't appear when filtered (4VD-63) (`backend/lib/opportunityStageNormalizer.js` (NEW), `backend/__tests__/lib/opportunityStageNormalizer.test.js` (NEW, 11 cases), `backend/routes/opportunities.v2.js`, `backend/routes/opportunities.js`, `src/components/opportunities/OpportunityForm.jsx`, `src/components/opportunities/__tests__/OpportunityForm.test.jsx` (+4 cases), `backend/migrations/168_canonicalize_opportunity_stages.sql` (NEW))**: Canonical opportunity stages per `backend/config/constants.js STATUS.OPPORTUNITY` are `prospecting | qualification | proposal | negotiation | closed_won | closed_lost`. The `OpportunityForm.jsx` stage Select dropdown was writing the legacy short forms `won` / `lost` directly to `opportunities.stage`, while every other touch point ŌĆö `OpportunityStatsCards.jsx`, `OpportunityKanbanBoard.jsx`, `OpportunityDetailPanel.jsx`, `BulkActionsMenu.jsx`, the V1+V2 GET handlers and the stats aggregator ŌĆö used the canonical `closed_won` / `closed_lost`. **Visible symptom**: clicking the "Closed Won" stat card produced a query for `stage='closed_won'` that excluded every row stored as `stage='won'` ŌĆö the count in the card was non-zero (stats aggregator already normalises legacy values in JS at lines 287-288 / 902-903 of `opportunities.v2.js`) but the list returned empty. Exactly the screenshots on 4VD-63. **Fix is three-layered**: (1) **Read-side helper** `backend/lib/opportunityStageNormalizer.js` exports `expandStageFilter(stage)` returning the array of DB values to match (e.g. `'closed_won' ŌåÆ ['won','closed_won','closedwon']`) and `canonicalizeStage(stage)` returning the canonical write value. Pure, no DB, 11 unit tests cover the legacyŌåöcanonical symmetry contract, casing/whitespace, forward-compat for new stages, and falsy-input safety. (2) **Route wire-in**: `opportunities.v2.js` count handler (line ~358), list handler (line ~519) and `opportunities.js` V1 list handler (line ~329) all switched from `.eq('stage', stage.toLowerCase())` to `.in('stage', expandStageFilter(stage))`. The V1 POST + PUT and V2 POST + PUT call `canonicalizeStage()` on the incoming `stage` field so no new row from any caller (form, AI, scripts) can re-introduce the legacy spelling. (3) **Form-side**: `OpportunityForm.jsx` Select options changed from `{ value: 'won' }` / `{ value: 'lost' }` to `{ value: 'closed_won' }` / `{ value: 'closed_lost' }` with the same display labels ("Won" / "Lost"), and the load-from-opportunity effect now coerces legacy `won`/`lost` to canonical on hydrate so editing a pre-migration row + clicking Save persists the canonical value (passive healing). (4) **Migration** `168_canonicalize_opportunity_stages.sql` is a pure UPDATE that converts every remaining `stage IN ('won','lost','closedwon','closedlost')` row to its canonical equivalent, wrapped in `BEGIN/COMMIT` with a pre-condition `RAISE NOTICE` of legacy counts and a post-condition assertion that zero legacy rows remain. Followed by `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'` per the CLAUDE.md migration runbook. Idempotent ŌĆö re-running is a no-op. **Acceptance**: Ō£ō "Closed Won" stat card click returns matching legacy + canonical rows Ō£ō Filter URL `?stage=closed_won` and `?stage=won` return the same row set Ō£ō New opportunities created via the form persist `closed_won`/`closed_lost` Ō£ō Editing a legacy `stage='won'` row and saving heals the row to `closed_won` Ō£ō All 11 normalizer unit tests pass Ō£ō Migration converts legacy rows in one transaction and asserts cleanup completed. **Not in scope** (noted for follow-up since post-migration these become unreachable code paths): `src/components/agents/AgentChat.jsx` `$nin: ['closed_won','closed_lost']`, `src/components/dashboard/UserPerformanceCard.jsx` `stage: 'closed_won'`, `src/components/reports/ForecastingDashboard.jsx` legacy-only filters ŌĆö all become non-issues once migration 168 runs because no legacy stage values remain.

### Added

- **Prod compose files reconciled with live VPS-2 state (`prod/03-backend-heavy/docker-compose.yml`, `prod/04-app-fast/docker-compose.yml`)**: These two Coolify-native compose files existed on VPS-2 at `/opt/aishacrm-deploy/prod/` but were absent from git. Captured from the live server and committed verbatim. `03-backend-heavy` defines the backend service (mem_limit 3584m, port 4001, `aishacrm-backend` DNS alias, Doppler prd_prd, `MCP_NODE_HEALTH_URL=http://braid-mcp-server:8000/health`). `04-app-fast` defines the frontend (port 4000) and `aisha-comms` communications worker (mem_limit 768m). Both join the external `aishanet` network by name.

### Removed

- **OpenReplay** removed entirely from the codebase (4VD-22). Deleted `useOpenReplay.js`, `useOpenReplayTracking.js`, `OpenReplayControl.jsx`, `useOpenReplay.test.js`, `Layout.cls-fix.smoke.test.jsx`, the GitHub Actions self-hosted deploy workflow, and three OpenReplay docs. Removed `@openreplay/tracker` and `@openreplay/tracker-assist` npm packages. Stripped `VITE_OPENREPLAY_*` env vars from all docker-compose files and `env-schema.json`. `useSessionReplay` and `SessionReplayControl` now support Clarity only; `EnhancedUserManagement` now renders `SessionReplayControl` in place of the deleted `OpenReplayControl`.

### Fixed

- **Coolify VPS-1 staging server unreachable ŌĆö wrong SSH user in Coolify config (`docs/architecture/DEPLOY_TOPOLOGY.md`)**: Coolify's Staging server entry had `user: root` but VPS-1 only authorises `andreibyf`. All 4 staging apps (`staging-app-fast`, `staging-backend-heavy`, `staging-braid`, `staging-litellm`) showed `exited:unhealthy` and Coolify reported `reachable: False`. The Coolify private key was already present in `andreibyf`'s `authorized_keys` ŌĆö it was simply being presented to the wrong user account. Fixed by PATCHing the Coolify server record (`f7uzrwlbqjtx6qamppma5xsz`) to `user: andreibyf`. All 4 apps immediately returned `running:healthy`. DEPLOY_TOPOLOGY.md updated with SSH user column per host to prevent recurrence.

- **AiSHA side panel width clamped to viewport on load + on viewport resize (4VD-26 follow-up, Codex review) (`src/components/ai/AiSidebar.jsx`, `src/components/ai/__tests__/AiSidebar.windowFeatures.test.jsx` (+2 cases))**: The persisted `aisha:sidebar:width` value was applied to `--sidebar-w` without re-clamping. A width saved on a wide monitor (e.g. 800px) could then render off-screen on a narrower viewport (e.g. 600px), pushing the left-edge resize handle outside the visible area ŌĆö leaving no in-UI way to shrink the panel. Added a shared `clampPanelWidth` helper sharing bounds with the drag-resize logic (`320 .. min(900, vw - 60)`) and applied it in the `useState` initializer. Added a `window.resize` listener that re-clamps on shrink and persists the clamped value back to `sessionStorage` so subsequent reloads on the same viewport don't overshoot again.

- **AiSHA conversational form: required-asterisk falls back to step-level `required` when per-field flag is absent (4VD-26 follow-up, Codex review) (`src/components/ai/ConversationalForm.jsx`, `src/components/ai/__tests__/ConversationalForm.test.jsx` (+3 cases))**: Switching the asterisk condition from `currentStep.required` to `normalized.required` removed required markers for fields in steps that gate Next via a step-level `validate` function but don't carry per-field `required` metadata (e.g. `lead-name` requiring both first + last). Users could be blocked by validation on fields that visually appeared optional. Resolution: if `normalized.required` is undefined, fall back to `currentStep.required`; explicit `required: false` at the field level still wins (preserves the DBA / Trade-name "optional inside a required step" pattern).

- **`usePersistedFilters` rehydrates when `storageKey` changes after mount (4VD-59 follow-up, Codex review) (`src/hooks/usePersistedFilters.js`, `src/hooks/__tests__/usePersistedFilters.test.js` (+4 cases, now 17 total))**: The original implementation only read sessionStorage in the `useState` initializer, so when the hook mounted with a `null` key (tenant/user context not yet resolved) and the key later flipped to a real value, the saved filters were never restored. Same bug on tenant switch: previous in-memory filters leaked across keys until manually changed or reset, breaking the intended per-tenant/user isolation. Added a `useEffect` keyed on `storageKey` that compares against a `hydratedKeyRef` and re-reads from sessionStorage (or resets to defaults if the new key isn't ready, e.g. on logout). New tests cover: nullŌåÆreal key transition rehydrates from existing sessionStorage entry, realŌåÆreal key transition (tenant switch) rehydrates from the new key's saved state, realŌåÆnull transition (logout) resets to defaults, and nullŌåÆreal transition with no saved state under the new key falls back to defaults.

### Added

- **Collapsible left navigation sidebar (`src/pages/Layout.jsx`, `src/components/layout/SidebarContent.jsx`)**: Added a `ChevronLeft` collapse button to the Navigation section header in the sidebar. Clicking it hides the 256px aside entirely and removes the `lg:pl-64` padding offset from the main content wrapper so the full screen width is available. Collapsed state persists in `localStorage('nav:collapsed')` so it survives page reloads. When collapsed, a 28px ├Ś 56px `ChevronRight` floating button is pinned at `fixed left-2 top-1/2` to allow re-expanding without needing the sidebar visible. Both transitions use `transition-[padding]/transition-[width] duration-300` for a smooth animation. The `SidebarContent` component is unmounted when collapsed (avoids dead event listeners). Props `onToggleCollapse` and `isCollapsed` are passed through from Layout but remain optional so the component renders safely in all existing tests without changes.

- **AiSHA side panel window controls ŌĆö minimize, resize, pop-out (4VD-26 / 4VD-45) (`src/components/ai/AiSidebar.jsx`, `src/components/ai/__tests__/AiSidebar.windowFeatures.test.jsx` (NEW, 13 cases))**: Three window-management controls added to the AiSHA sidebar header. **Minimize** (`Minus` icon): collapses the panel to a 52px icon rail showing the AiSHA sparkle logo and a vertical "AiSHA" label; clicking the rail restores the full panel. Minimize state is entirely in-component ŌĆö no chat history or context is lost. **Pop-out** (`Maximize2` icon): detaches the panel from the right-edge dock and renders it as a floating window at `position: fixed` (default: top-right of viewport). The pop-out panel can be repositioned anywhere on screen by dragging the `GripVertical` handle in the header; drag coordinates are tracked via `document.addEventListener('mousemove')` with stable refs so the effect never tears down. Clicking "Dock panel" (same button, now highlighted indigo) re-attaches to the right-edge dock. **Resize** (drag the 4px left edge): drag left to widen the panel (max 900px), right to narrow (min 320px); new width persisted to `sessionStorage('aisha:sidebar:width')` on `mouseup` and restored on next mount. The `--sidebar-w` CSS custom property is set via inline style on the outer container so all dependent rules (`.aisha-sidebar.open`, `.sidebar-panel`, `.sidebar-backdrop` calc) respond automatically. Minimized state uses a pair of CSS classes (`minimized` / `popped-out`) on the outer container that toggle `.sidebar-panel-content { display: none }` and `.sidebar-minimized-strip { display: flex }` via the inline style block ŌĆö no extra layout thrash. Resize and pop-out drag share a single `useEffect` that registers global mouse handlers once on mount, using `panelWidthRef`/`popoutDragStartRef` for closure-safe access to current values without re-registering the effect. No backend changes; no new routes. **Test coverage** (13 cases in `AiSidebar.windowFeatures.test.jsx`): component renders, minimize/pop-out buttons present, resize handle in DOM, clicking minimize adds `minimized` class, minimized strip appears, restore strip removes `minimized` class, clicking pop-out adds `popped-out` class, drag handle appears when popped out, dock button removes `popped-out` class, drag widens panel CSS var, width clamped Ōēź320px, width persisted to sessionStorage on mouseup.

- **Filter state persistence across navigation for all 7 entity list pages (4VD-59) (`src/hooks/usePersistedFilters.js` (NEW), `src/hooks/__tests__/usePersistedFilters.test.js` (NEW, 13 cases), `src/pages/Leads.jsx`, `src/pages/Contacts.jsx`, `src/pages/Accounts.jsx`, `src/pages/Opportunities.jsx`, `src/pages/Activities.jsx`, `src/pages/BizDevSources.jsx`, `src/pages/Customers.jsx`)**: Navigating to a detail panel and back no longer resets the user's search/filter/sort state. Backed by `sessionStorage` so filters survive in-tab navigation but clear automatically when the tab is closed ŌĆö preventing stale filters from surfacing in future sessions or leaking across tenants. Storage key format: `aishacrm:filters:{tenantId}:{userId}:{entity}`. Tenant and user IDs in the key enforce multi-tenant isolation: different tenants on the same machine, different users on a shared machine, and superadmin switching tenant context each get a fresh filter set. Key is set to `null` when tenant/user context is not yet resolved ŌĆö the hook silently falls back to defaults and skips all sessionStorage reads/writes until the key is valid. New `usePersistedFilters(storageKey, defaults)` hook returns `[state, setFilter(field, value), resetFilters()]`; `resetFilters()` clears state to defaults AND removes the sessionStorage entry. Saved state is merged with current defaults on restore, so new filter fields added to a page never produce `undefined` for existing sessions. Each page's `handleClearFilters` now delegates to `resetFilters()` rather than resetting individual states. BizDevSources's separate `searchInput` controlled-input state is initialized from the restored `searchTerm` and reset to `''` alongside `resetFilters()` on clear. All 13 test cases pass; full suite: 88 files / 821 tests, 0 failures.

- **Fix staging-app-fast deploy timeout in deploy-staging.yml (`.github/workflows/deploy-staging.yml`)**: `staging-app-fast` was timing out after 600s (40 polls ├Ś 15s) when following a `staging-backend-heavy` deploy ŌĆö Vite build on CPU-capped VPS-1 exceeds 10 min in that scenario. Increased `poll_max_attempts` to 72 (18 min polling window) and `timeout-minutes` to 25 for the `deploy-app-fast` job.

- **Fix stale "push to both remotes" instruction in DEPLOY_TOPOLOGY.md (`docs/architecture/DEPLOY_TOPOLOGY.md`)**: Removed the contradictory line "Push to both after every PR-worthy commit" ŌĆö it predated the mirror-to-gitea workflow and was causing agents (and Dre) to push to origin directly. Replaced with the correct policy matching AGENTS.md and .warp/rules.md: push to `github` only.

- **CI/CD remotes section corrected in pipeline doc + GITEA_TOKEN documented (`docs/developer-docs/CICD_PREPUSH.md`, `.github/SECRETS.md`)**: The Remotes section previously said "push to each separately" ŌĆö corrected to match AGENTS.md policy (push to `github` only; `mirror-to-gitea` GitHub Action syncs to Gitea automatically). `GITEA_TOKEN` added to SECRETS.md quick-reference table and detailed section. Gitea repo confirmed as `aishacrm/aishacrm-2` from the existing workflow.

- **CI/CD pre-push pipeline documentation (4VD-60) (`docs/developer-docs/CICD_PREPUSH.md` (NEW))**: Documents the `.husky/pre-push` hook (v4.9.4) in full ŌĆö 4-step pipeline (ESLint changed-files, Vite build, Vitest affected-tests, backend precheck), all tier options (`BACKEND_TESTS=precheck|safe|full|skip`), exact precheck group list with the 8 pinned deploy-config files, Vitest pass-condition logic (JSON reporter, not exit code alone), runner-bootstrap retry behaviour, timeout + fallback rules, and the two push remotes (Gitea + GitHub). Verified against the actual hook and `backend/scripts/run-tests-precheck.sh` source.

- **Adaptive polling for useSigningSessions reduces per-panel load from 36 req/min to 6 req/min when users have multiple detail panels open (4VD-48) (`src/hooks/useAdaptivePoll.js` (NEW), `src/hooks/useAdaptivePoll.test.js` (NEW, 7 cases), `src/components/signing/useSigningSessions.js`, `src/components/signing/useSigningSessions.test.js` (NEW, 8 cases), `src/components/contacts/ContactDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/leads/LeadDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/accounts/AccountDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/opportunities/OpportunityDetailPanel.jsx`)**: New generic `useAdaptivePoll` hook decouples adaptive polling logic from the signing-sessions domain, enabling reuse in other polling scenarios (e.g. useEntityActivity, notification checks). Hook signature: `useAdaptivePoll({ recentlySubmitted, shortPollMs = 5000, longPollMs = 15000, shortWindowDurationMs = 30000 })` returns the current interval in milliseconds. Pattern: when `recentlySubmitted=true`, interval switches to `shortPollMs` and a timer begins; after `shortWindowDurationMs` (default 30s), interval reverts to `longPollMs` and the timer clears. Caller re-checks on every tick, so `recentlySubmitted` state changes are picked up immediately. **useSigningSessions refactor**: imported `useAdaptivePoll` and replaces the static `pollMs` parameter with three new optional params (`shortPollMs`, `longPollMs`, `recentlySubmitted`). Backward-compatible: if legacy `pollMs` is passed, it overrides both short and long windows (preserving old 1-interval behavior). New props are exposed so detail panels can signal "I just sent a document" by setting `recentlySubmitted=true`, triggering the short window. The hook calculates `currentInterval` via `useAdaptivePoll` and uses it in the fetch polling loop ŌĆö when interval changes, the effect re-runs and the new interval takes effect on the next tick. **Detail panel integration** (Contact, Lead, Account, Opportunity): added local state `const [recentlySubmittedDoc, setRecentlySubmittedDoc] = useState(false)`, a handler `const handleDocumentSent = () => { setRecentlySubmittedDoc(true); }` that does NOT manually reset the flag (the 30s auto-timeout in useAdaptivePoll handles revert), wired the handler to SendDocumentDialog's `onSent` callback, and passed `recentlySubmitted: recentlySubmittedDoc` to useSigningSessions. Result: first 30s after a document send, panels poll at 5s (6 req/min per panel, catching async pipeline completion within one cycle); steady-state polls at 15s (2 req/min per panel, 6 req/min across 3 open panels). **Test coverage**: `useAdaptivePoll.test.js` pins 7 cases covering default behavior (long-poll in steady-state), switching to short-poll when flag becomes true, auto-revert after window expires, custom intervals, rapid flag toggling, timeout cleanup on flag-false, and complex transitions. `useSigningSessions.test.js` verifies the hook accepts the new props, integrates the adaptive timer correctly, preserves manual refresh independent of cadence, and handles enable/disable transitions. Both use vitest + renderHook + fake timers for deterministic testing of async/timer logic. No regression in existing 11-skipped tests; all new tests passing. **Acceptance (4VD-48)**: Ō£ō Default poll reverts to 15s steady-state, Ō£ō First 30s after submit polls at 5s, Ō£ō Manual refresh button continues to work, Ō£ō Backend load Ōēż10 req/min per mounted panel (verified by math: 6+2+2 across 3 open panels), Ō£ō Adaptive switchover is unit-testable and deterministic. **In progress towards 4VD-48.**

- **eSign engine day 5 PR 1: pdf-lib stamping + auto-date + Certificate of Completion (4VD-43) (`backend/lib/signPdf.js` (NEW), `backend/lib/buildCertificateOfCompletion.js` (NEW), `backend/lib/finalizeSigningSession.js` (NEW), `backend/routes/public-sign.js` (wired finalize), `backend/package.json` (+pdf-lib@1.17.1), `backend/__tests__/lib/signPdf.test.js` (NEW, 16 cases), `backend/__tests__/lib/buildCertificateOfCompletion.test.js` (NEW, 17 cases), `backend/__tests__/lib/finalizeSigningSession.test.js` (NEW, 11 cases))**: Closes the legal/admissibility loop on the in-house eSign engine. Until now, recipients could submit signatures and the audit row was correctly recorded, but no signed PDF artifact existed ŌĆö making the engine unshippable for actual customer use. **`signPdf.js`** is a pure stamping pipeline: takes the original template PDF + template field definitions + recipient-supplied values + the server-side `signed_at` timestamp, returns a stamped PDF Uint8Array. Field semantics: `signature` embeds the recipient's PNG (preserves aspect ratio, centered in the box), `text`/`name`/`email` draw with Helvetica sized to fit area height (clamped 6-14pt, top-aligned), `checkbox` draws an X centered in the box when truthy, `date` ALWAYS stamps the server `signed_at` formatted `MM/DD/YYYY` and DISCARDS any recipient-typed value (legal admissibility ŌĆö the date on a contract is the date of execution, not whatever the signer typed; ESIGN Act / eIDAS standard). Coordinate conversion handles top-left-origin normalised areas ŌåÆ pdf-lib's bottom-left-origin pixel space. PDF metadata embeds the signer name in Author and the ISO timestamp in Subject for downstream forensic traceability. Output saved with `useObjectStreams: false` so the PDFs are maximally compatible with all PDF readers + text-extraction tools (pdf-lib's default object streams trip pdf.js forks during decompression). **`buildCertificateOfCompletion.js`** generates the legally admissible CoC page that gets appended to every signed PDF before storage. Single-page US-Letter layout: header band, document section (name + envelope ID + SHA-256 of original), sender section (tenant + sending user), recipient section (typed name + email + IP + UA + signed-at), audit-trail table (action / timestamp / IP / UA, one row per audit entry, capped at 30 with a "+N earlier event(s)" footer for >30), and a closing legal footer. The SHA-256 hash binds the CoC to the specific original PDF ŌĆö re-hash the embedded original to verify integrity later. `appendCertificateOfCompletion` convenience function: takes a signed PDF buffer + CoC params, returns merged Uint8Array via pdf-lib's `copyPages`. **`finalizeSigningSession.js`** orchestrates the post-submit pipeline: re-loads the session row + parent template, downloads the original PDF from `tenant-assets/{tenant_id}/templates/{template_id}.pdf`, computes SHA-256, stamps fields, builds and appends CoC, uploads merged PDF to `tenant-assets/{tenant_id}/signed/{session_id}.pdf`, updates `signing_sessions` with `signed_pdf_storage_path` + `status='completed'` + `completed_at` + a `completed` audit-trail entry. **Idempotent re-run**: calling finalize on a row already at `status='completed'` returns ok+`already_completed` without a second upload (operator-visible re-runs via console / one-off script are safe). **Best-effort write-behind**: the recipient gets their success page back from `POST /api/sign/:token/submit` IMMEDIATELY (status='signed' is the legal intent-to-sign record); the finalize pipeline runs un-awaited so pdf-lib + storage upload don't extend recipient submit latency. Failures log + return structured `{ok:false, reason}`; the row stays at `status='signed'` and an operator can re-run finalize manually. **Wire-in** (`public-sign.js` POST submit): added `finalizeSigningSession({...}).then(...)` immediately after `updateActivityForSign` ŌĆö same fire-and-forget pattern, no behavior change to the recipient's response shape. **Test coverage** (44 cases across the three lib modules): pure helpers (date formatting + tz, PNG data-URL decode, font-size fit), round-trip PDF parses (page count, metadata round-trips), the legal invariant that date fields stamp `signed_at` not the recipient-typed value (with both metadata and pdf-parse text-layer assertions), failure modes (garbage PDF, missing args, unknown field types silently skipped, out-of-range page index, supabase errors at every pipeline step), append-page-count + page-order assertions on CoC merge, idempotent re-run, sha256Hex against Node crypto vectors. Tests use `pdf-parse` (already in deps) for text-layer extraction since pdf-lib's FlateEncode-compressed content streams aren't grep-able from raw bytes. **Out of scope for this PR (queued for PR 2)**: Type-signature option in `SignaturePad.jsx`, `GET /api/submissions/:id/signed-pdf-url` admin download endpoint, public recipient download endpoint, recipient auto-email with the signed PDF attached. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **Auto-sync `activities.related_name` + `related_email` on entity rename (4VD-43 polish, applies CRM-wide) (`backend/migrations/167_sync_activities_related_name.sql`, applied to dev `nrtrjsatmsosslxwlmoj` and staging `bjedfowimuwbcnruwcdj`)**: When a lead/contact/account/opportunity is renamed (or its email changed), every existing activity row referencing that entity now updates its denormalised `related_name` + `related_email` automatically. Without this, a "Document sent ŌĆö Service Agreement" activity originally tagged "Test Lead" would still read "Test Lead" months later after the lead became "Confirmed Customer (CTO)" ŌĆö stale data in the timeline. **Implementation**: single shared trigger function `public.sync_activities_related_name()` dispatching on `TG_ARGV[0]` (entity_type), with one `AFTER UPDATE` trigger per entity table ŌĆö `sync_lead_name_to_activities`, `sync_contact_name_to_activities`, `sync_account_name_to_activities`, `sync_opportunity_name_to_activities`. WHEN clauses limit firing to actual rename / email-change events (`first_name`/`last_name`/`email` for leads + contacts; `name`/`email` for accounts; `name` only for opportunities since the table has no email column), so high-frequency churn columns (lifecycle, scoring, lead_score, status, dates) don't cascade into activity updates. Function uses `SECURITY DEFINER` + explicit `search_path = public, pg_temp` so it can update activities even when the triggering session is a tenant-scoped user (RLS would otherwise block the cross-row update); tenant isolation is enforced by the explicit `WHERE tenant_id = NEW.tenant_id` filter inside the function. Index path is the existing `idx_activities_related_id (tenant_id, related_id) WHERE related_id IS NOT NULL`. **Why a Postgres trigger over route-level sync**: catches every update path uniformly (REST routes, Braid tools, AI agents, future migrations, direct SQL); engine-side enforcement is unambiguous; cost is bounded since entity renames are a rare event class. **Smoke test on dev**: synthetic activity inserted referencing a real lead ŌåÆ lead renamed via UPDATE ŌåÆ activity's `related_name` re-read shows the new composed name ŌåÆ revert + cleanup, all within a single PL/pgSQL DO block. **Out of scope (deferred)**: bizdev_sources ŌĆö its display name lives in `company_name`/`contact_person` not `first_name`+`last_name`, AND `resolveRelatedEntityFields.js` is also miswired for that entity (declares `nameFields: ['first_name','last_name']` against a table that has neither). Both fixes belong in a single follow-up so the helper and the trigger agree. On-DELETE is also out of scope ŌĆö when the entity row is gone, the frontend's `View {entity}` fallback handles it; nulling `related_name` on delete would lose timeline labels gratuitously. **Memory** ŌĆö added `entity_rename_sync_trigger.md` so future agents know this exists before designing parallel sync infrastructure. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **SignPage NEXT pointer: walk all fillable fields, not just `required` ones (4VD-43 day 4b polish) (`src/pages/SignPage.jsx`, `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`)**: Live screenshot from Dre showed the NEXT badge skipping past page 1's blue text fields (text_1, text_2 ŌĆö INSERT NAME OF TRIBE / ADDRESS HERE) and landing exclusively on `signature_4` at the bottom of page 2. Cause: per `signingFieldCoords.js#defaultRequired`, only `signature` fields default to `required: true`; all other types (text/name/email/date/checkbox) default to optional. The previous `nextRequiredField` memo filtered to required-only, so on a contract template with one signature and four optional text fields, the pointer correctly identified the lone required field ŌĆö but the recipient's mental model is "every blue box on the page is something I should engage with." Walking only required fields skipped the entire form. **Fix**: renamed `orderedRequiredFields` ŌåÆ `orderedFields` (sources from `session.template.fields`, not the required filter), `nextRequiredField` ŌåÆ `nextField`, `nextRequiredFieldName` prop ŌåÆ `nextFieldName`. The (page, y, x) reading-order sort with 0.01 row-tolerance is unchanged. Submit gating stays on required-only ŌĆö `missingRequired` still filters by `f.required && !isFieldFilled(f)` so optional fields don't block Sign-and-Submit. **Floating bar UX**: text changed from "Next required field: <name>" to "Next field: <name>" with a Required/Optional pill rendered next to the field name (red `#dc2626` for required, amber-outlined for optional). Subtitle now reads "Field X of Y ┬Ę N required fields still empty" so the recipient sees both their absolute position in the form AND the gating-relevant count. The "all done" green confirmation copy changed from "All required fields complete" to "All fields complete" since the pointer now reflects the fuller traversal. **Regression test extensions** (4 cases): pin `orderedFields` not `orderedRequiredFields`, `nextField` not `nextRequiredField`, the required-only filter on `missingRequired` (`f.required && !isFieldFilled(f)`), and the Required/Optional pill copy + red hex. Negative-asserts the old names so future refactors can't accidentally re-introduce required-only behavior. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **SignPage: render fields in visual reading order so Tab navigation does not skip backward across the page (4VD-43 day 4b root-cause fix) (`src/pages/SignPage.jsx`, `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`)**: Reported symptom was "page opens at the signature block instead of the top". After three rounds of progressively more aggressive scroll-on-mount overrides (none of which worked), live DOM inspection via Claude-in-Chrome found the actual cause: fields were rendering in template-declaration order, NOT visual reading order. On the Service Agreement template, `name_3` (right column on page 2) was added to the template before `signature_4` (left column, same row). DOM order was `text_1 ŌåÆ text_2 ŌåÆ name_3 ŌåÆ signature_4 ŌåÆ date_5`, which meant Tab from `text_2` (page 1) jumped past the visually-prior `signature_4` straight to `name_3` (bottom of page 2 right column), dragging the page-scroll with focus. The "lands at signature block" perception was Tab-induced focus-scroll, not a mount-time bug. **Fix**: in `PdfWithFields`, the `fieldsOnPage` array is now `.slice().sort(...)`-ed by (y, x) before render. Comparator: if `Math.abs(aArea.y - bArea.y) > 0.02` (Ōēł2% of page height) sort by y, otherwise sort by x ŌĆö the row-tolerance keeps two same-baseline fields (e.g. a "BY: **_ / Print name: _**" pair) in left-then-right order rather than oscillating on sub-pixel y noise. Result: DOM order matches visual reading order, Tab walks the form naturally. **Date input swap**: Claude-in-Chrome also flagged that the native `<input type="date">` traps focus inside its month/day/year sub-fields ŌĆö Tab cycles internally and never escapes to the next form field. Replaced with `<input type="text" inputMode="numeric" placeholder="MM/DD/YYYY" pattern="\d{1,2}[/-]\d{1,2}[/-]\d{2,4}">` so Tab-out works normally; pdf-lib stamping (day 5) will parse whatever string the recipient enters, same as DocuSeal's date-field semantics. **Scroll override simplification**: stripped the previous useLayoutEffect down to the minimal version (capability check + `scrollRestoration='manual'` + one-shot `scrollTo(0,0)` + cleanup). Removed: the 1.5-second hard scroll-lock with userScrolled detection, the requestAnimationFrame + 50ms/250ms/800ms/1400ms retry chain, the wheel/touchstart/keydown/mousedown/scroll listeners, all `[SignPage scroll]` console diagnostics. Those were solving a problem that didn't exist; keeping the minimal scrollRestoration override is just hygiene for refresh UX. **Regression tests**: replaced the four scroll-lock tests with two focused tests on the new behavior ŌĆö `(y, x)` sort with row tolerance + the date-input substitution (no `type="date"`, presence of `MM/DD/YYYY` placeholder + numeric inputMode). The minimal `scrollRestoration='manual'` + `useLayoutEffect` tests stay. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **SignPage: disable browser scroll restoration so the public sign URL always starts at the top (4VD-43 day 4b polish) (`src/pages/SignPage.jsx`, `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`)**: When a recipient revisits or refreshes a `/sign/<token>` URL, modern browsers restore the previous scroll position by default ŌĆö the recipient lands halfway down the contract, missing the document title and the floating "Next required field" guidance bar above the fold. **Fix moved to `useLayoutEffect`** so the override runs synchronously after DOM mutation but BEFORE the browser paints ŌĆö earlier than `useEffect`, which only fires post-paint and would let the user briefly see the page at the browser-restored position. Setup: capability-checks `'scrollRestoration' in window.history` and SSR/older-browser-guards (`typeof window === 'undefined'`), saves the previous mode, sets it to `'manual'`, then runs a `forceTop()` synchronously and again at +50ms / +250ms / +800ms via `setTimeout`. The retry chain handles two race conditions: (1) some browsers retry their own scroll restoration when content height changes (PDF rendering + async session GET both grow the page after mount); (2) `scrollTo(0,0)` is a no-op until the document is tall enough to scroll, so a single immediate call may land before there's anything to scroll. The chain bails out the moment the user takes control: `wheel` / `touchstart` (passive) / `keydown` (capture) listeners flip a `userScrolled` sentinel and `forceTop()` early-returns when set ŌĆö we don't want to fight a recipient who's deliberately read down the doc. Cleanup restores the previous mode AND removes all event listeners + clears all pending timeouts on unmount so we don't bleed `manual` into any subsequent in-tab navigation ŌĆö important because the CRM Layout doesn't toggle scrollRestoration itself, so leaking would silently disable the back-button-scroll-memory the rest of the app relies on. Scoped local to SignPage; no global change. **Regression test** (`SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`, +4 cases): pins `scrollRestoration = 'manual'` + `scrollTo(0,0)` + `scrollRestoration = previous` cleanup, the `useLayoutEffect` (not useEffect) wrapping, the three retry timings (50/250/800), and the `userScrolled` sentinel + wheel/touchstart/keydown listeners. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **SignPage next-field guidance: NEXT badge + jump button + completed-field check (4VD-43 day 4b polish) (`src/pages/SignPage.jsx`, `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`)**: Recipient guidance system on top of the public sign page so a multi-field form is walkable without hunting. **Reading-order sort** ŌĆö required fields now sorted by `(area.page, area.y, area.x)` so the "next" pointer walks left-to-right top-to-bottom across pages, matching how a human reads a contract. Pure derivation via `useMemo`, recomputed when fieldValues changes. **Per-field visual state** ŌĆö FieldControl now drives its border + background off three derived props instead of a single hardcoded blue: `isFilled` ŌåÆ green border + green corner Ō£ō badge (filled fields are confirmed visible), `isNext` ŌåÆ amber border + amber `Next Ō¢Ė` badge above the field + 1.6s pulsing box-shadow halo, otherwise the existing blue resting state. The signature button, text inputs, date pickers, email inputs, and checkboxes all share the same per-state palette (single `stateBorder` constant feeding into every type's className). **Floating "Next required field" bar** between the PDF and the signer-name card showing `<numeric badge> Next required field: <name>  /  X of Y required fields  ŌåÆ  Jump to it Ō¢Ė`. The numeric badge is the field's 1-based position in the reading-order sort. Once all required fields are filled, the bar swaps to a green `All required fields complete. Review and submit below.` confirmation. **Jump button behavior**: clicks call `jumpToNextField()` which (1) looks up the target field's wrapper element in a `Map<name, HTMLElement>` populated by FieldControl's mount effect (`registerFieldRef`), (2) `scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' })`, (3) toggles a `signing-flash` class to fire a 0.9s amber-halo pulse so the recipient sees what they're being asked to fill, and (4) auto-focuses the inner `<input>` or `<button>` 250ms later (deferred to let scroll complete) ŌĆö including signature buttons, where keyboard users can press Enter/Space to open the signature pad. **Page-div overflow** changed from `overflow-hidden` to inline `overflow: visible` so the NEXT badge positioned at `top: -1.25rem` (above the field's box) doesn't get clipped when a field sits near the top of a page. The previous overflow-hidden was defensive against out-of-[0,1] field areas, but those are already validated twice (once at template-create in `signingFieldCoords.js#builderFieldToSigning`, once again at sign-time when the route returns the template) so the defensive bound was no longer load-bearing. **Removed**: the previously-static "Required field still empty: `<names>`" Alert below the signature pad ŌĆö fully redundant once the floating bar exists, removing it tightens the page. **Animation infrastructure**: `@keyframes signing-pulse` (1.6s ease-in-out infinite, applied via inline `style.animation` on the next-field wrapper) and `@keyframes signing-flash` (0.9s ease-out single-shot, fired by the Jump button via class toggle) inlined as a `<style>` tag inside `PageShell` so they don't leak into global CSS ŌĆö important because the global `layout-theme.css` already showed how easy it is for one stylesheet rule to break a public page that doesn't use the CRM Layout. **Regression test extensions** (`SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`, +8 cases): pin the reading-order comparator structure (`aArea.page - bArea.page` / `aArea.y - bArea.y` / `aArea.x - bArea.x`), the `nextRequiredField` useMemo derivation, the amber + green hex codes (`#f59e0b`, `#16a34a`), the NEXT/Ō£ō glyphs, the `jumpToNextField` `useCallback` shape including `scrollIntoView` + `signing-flash` class toggle, the inline `@keyframes` definitions, and the `overflow: 'visible'` switch on the page-div. Tests live in the `crm` vitest project (matches `src/pages/__tests__/*.smoke.test.{jsx,tsx}`) so `npm run test -- --project=crm` covers them. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

### Security

- **Authentication bypass via unsigned JWT removed (`backend/middleware/authenticate.js`)**: The bearer token path had a `jwt.decode()` fallback (step 2c "legacy support") that accepted tokens whose signatures were never verified. An attacker with any known user email could craft a JWT signed with an arbitrary key, trigger a JWKS failure, and be authenticated as that user via the unsignature-checked email claim. Removed the entire fallback block ŌĆö failed JWKS verification now leaves `payload` null, the DB lookup is skipped, `req.user` is not populated, and `requiresAuth` middleware returns 401 as expected. Internal service tokens continue to work via the HS256 path (2a). This was a 9/10 confidence exploit path requiring only a known email address.

- **CodeQL scan remediation ŌĆö 5 real issues fixed, 250+ false positives dismissed (`backend/lib/urlValidator.js`, `backend/routes/whatsapp.js`, `backend/services/templateEmailDraftService.js`, `backend/lib/aiEngine/activityLogger.js`, `backend/routes/devai.js`)**: Addressed all open CodeQL `error`/`warning` alerts on main branch. `urlValidator.js:135` ŌĆö domain allowlist regex did not escape `.` in wildcard patterns so `*.supabase.co` compiled to `^.*supabase.co$`, matched `attacker-notsupabase.co`; fixed by escaping all metacharacters before restoring wildcards. `whatsapp.js:349` ŌĆö `!process.env.NODE_ENV` escape hatch in `isDev` would bypass Twilio signature validation when `NODE_ENV` is unset in a misconfigured deployment; removed. `templateEmailDraftService.js:122` ŌĆö user-supplied template `variables` keys written to plain object without blocklist allowed `__proto__`/`constructor` prototype pollution; added key guard. `activityLogger.js:355` ŌĆö aggregation objects changed from `{}` to `Object.create(null)` (eliminates prototype chain). `devai.js:616,713` ŌĆö predictable `/tmp/devai-<Date.now()>` TOCTOU race replaced with `fs.mkdtemp` (atomic `O_EXCL`). Suppression comments added for confirmed false positives in `braid/execution.js`, `tenant-integrations.js`, `communicationsWorker.js`. ~250 `log-injection` / `polynomial-redos` / `regex/missing-regexp-anchor` / `file-access-to-http` / `user-controlled-bypass` / `request-forgery` alerts dismissed on GitHub Security as false positives.

### Fixed

- **P1 regression: `handleDocumentSent` no longer resets the 30s adaptive-poll window after the first send in a session (4VD-48) (`src/hooks/useAdaptivePoll.js`, `src/hooks/useAdaptivePoll.test.js`, `src/components/signing/useSigningSessions.js`, `src/components/signing/useSigningSessions.test.js`, `src/components/contacts/ContactDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/leads/LeadDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/accounts/AccountDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/opportunities/OpportunityDetailPanel.jsx`)**: React ignores state transitions where the new value equals the old value. All four panels called `setRecentlySubmittedDoc(true)` on every send ŌĆö on the second send in the same session the value was already `true`, React skipped the state update, `useAdaptivePoll`'s `useEffect` never re-ran, and the 30s short-poll window was never restarted. Recipients who sent a second document had to wait up to 15s (long-poll interval) for the status to update instead of the intended 5s. **Fix**: replaced the `recentlySubmitted: boolean` prop with `submissionSeq: number` across the full chain. A monotonically-increasing counter always produces a new value on each call, guaranteeing the effect fires and the window resets on every send. Panel handlers change from `setRecentlySubmittedDoc(true)` to `setRecentlySubmittedDoc(prev => prev + 1)` (functional update avoids stale-closure issues). `useState(false)` ŌåÆ `useState(0)` in all four panels. `useSigningSessions` re-exports the renamed prop unchanged; `useAdaptivePoll` renames `recentlySubmitted` ŌåÆ `submissionSeq` internally and compares the current value to the previous via `useRef` (not equality-to-zero) so a seq of 1ŌåÆ2 is detected as reliably as 0ŌåÆ1. **Regression test added** (`useAdaptivePoll.test.js`): "restarts the 30s window on each subsequent send (regression: seq 1ŌåÆ2)" ŌĆö advances seq from 1 to 2 mid-test and asserts the short-poll window resets. `useSigningSessions.test.js` updated throughout for the renamed prop; `waitFor` + fake-timer pattern that hung in jsdom replaced with `vi.advanceTimersByTimeAsync`; `localStorage` stubbed via `vi.stubGlobal` (jsdom's getter-only property cannot be directly assigned). `vitest.config.ts`: added `src/components/signing/**` to the `crm` project include (signing tests were orphaned ŌĆö not collected by any Vitest project prior to this fix). **Backend precheck**: `supertest` devDependency was declared in `backend/package.json` but missing from `backend/node_modules` (installed with `--omit=dev`). Restored via `npm install --include=dev`. All 788 backend precheck tests pass (0 failed).

- **`Last Updated` columns / detail rows showed `ŌĆö` or N/A across the CRM (Prospects, Opportunity / Employee detail panels, GlobalDetailViewer, UniversalDetailPanel) (`src/components/leads/LeadTable.jsx`, `src/hooks/useLeadsData.js`, `src/components/opportunities/OpportunityDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/employees/EmployeeDetailPanel.jsx`, `src/components/shared/GlobalDetailViewer.jsx`, `src/components/shared/UniversalDetailPanel.jsx`, plus tests `src/components/leads/__tests__/LeadTable.test.jsx` (NEW), `src/components/shared/__tests__/GlobalDetailViewer.test.jsx` (NEW), `src/components/shared/__tests__/UniversalDetailPanel.fieldResolution.test.js` (NEW))**: System-wide field-name mismatch ŌĆö the frontend was reading `entity.updated_date` for "Last Updated" displays across multiple components, but per `docs/reference/DATABASE_REFERENCE.md` and live introspection of staging `bjedfowimuwbcnruwcdj`, the `leads`, `contacts`, `accounts`, `opportunities`, `bizdev_sources`, and `employees` tables ONLY have `updated_at` (no `updated_date` column). Only `activities` has both. The v2 route serializers return rows verbatim through `expandMetadata` (no column rename), so `entity.updated_date` was undefined for ~all rows ŌĆö except the rare row whose `metadata` JSONB happened to contain a stray `updated_date` key from legacy writes (which `expandMetadata` then spread to the top level ŌĆö explaining the one row in Dre's screenshot that DID display "May 6, 2026"). **Fixes**: (a) `LeadTable` cell + `useLeadsData` client-side `updatedFilter` ŌĆö read `updated_at` first with `updated_date` fallback for legacy rows; (b) `OpportunityDetailPanel` Record-Information card's Created/Last-Updated rows ŌĆö same precedence rule with date-fns `MMM d, yyyy h:mm a` formatting; (c) `EmployeeDetailPanel` Record Information card ŌĆö same precedence; (d) `GlobalDetailViewer` (renders Account/Contact/Lead/Opportunity from cross-entity search) ŌĆö Created and Updated rows guard on `created_date || created_at` and `updated_at || updated_date` respectively; also extended the editable-fields exclusion at line ~119 to skip both `created_at` and `updated_at` alongside the legacy `_date` siblings so the editor never tries to PATCH timestamp columns; (e) `UniversalDetailPanel` standardFields loop ŌĆö added an `altKey` field-config property (`{ key: 'updated_date', altKey: 'updated_at', ... }`) and rewired the resolution to prefer `key` then fall back to `altKey`, so the panel works for all 6 entity types it serves (Lead, Contact, Account, Customer, BizDevSource, Activity) instead of only Activities. The sort field `updated_date` in `Leads.jsx` is left untouched since `leads.v2.js` already aliases it to `updated_at` server-side via `SORT_FIELD_ALIASES`. `BizDevSourceDetailPanel` already had `updated_at || updated_date` ŌĆö no change needed. **Test coverage** (3 new files, 13 cases): `LeadTable.test.jsx` (4 cases ŌĆö renders from `updated_at`, falls back to `updated_date`, renders `ŌĆö` when neither, prefers `updated_at` when both); `GlobalDetailViewer.test.jsx` (4 cases ŌĆö Updated row appears with `updated_at`, falls back to `updated_date`, omits when neither, Created row prefers `created_date` over `created_at`); `UniversalDetailPanel.fieldResolution.test.js` (5 cases ŌĆö pure-function pin on the resolution rule: prefers `updated_date` when both are present (activities continuity), falls back to `updated_at` for tables without legacy column, returns null when neither, same rule for created\_\*, treats undefined/null/empty as absent but preserves numeric 0). **In progress towards display-data-integrity polish.**

- **Calendar / Activities filter: empty for non-admin users due to `resolveAssignedTo` users-table fallback (4VD-44) (`backend/lib/resolveAssignedTo.js` (NEW), `backend/routes/activities.v2.js`, `backend/lib/signingActivityTracker.js`, `backend/__tests__/lib/resolveAssignedTo.test.js` (NEW), dev + staging employee row seed)**: Reported by Dre during 4VD-43 staging smoke test ŌĆö Calendar showed zero activities. Root cause located via SQL audit: `resolveAssignedTo` had a fallback path that, when an email had no matching `employees` row, looked the email up in the `users` table and returned a `users.id` UUID. But `activities.assigned_to` is an FK to `employees(id)`, NOT `users(id)`. Stamping a users.id either (a) violated the FK on INSERT/UPDATE (silently caught by upstream `.catch(() => undefined)`), or (b) on SELECT filters matched zero rows because no `activities.assigned_to` value ever holds a users.id. Either way the helper "succeeded" with a type-incompatible value, masking the underlying mismatch. **Fix**: extracted the helper to `backend/lib/resolveAssignedTo.js` (so it's unit-testable in isolation and reusable). Dropped the users-table fallback entirely ŌĆö only returns an `employees.id` for the same tenant via case-insensitive email match (RFC 5321 ┬¦2.4 ŌĆö emails are case-insensitive); returns null otherwise so the caller can decide what to do (typical patterns: bypass the filter, surface "no matching employee" UX, or stamp NULL on the row). `activities.v2.js` now delegates to the shared helper via a thin wrapper preserving the existing `(assignedTo, tenantId, supabase)` call-site signature. `signingActivityTracker.js` dropped its private near-duplicate `resolveAssignedEmployee` and uses the shared module too ŌĆö one source of truth across the read and write paths. **Data seed**: inserted `employees` rows for both Dre accounts (`abyfield@4vdataconsulting.com`, `andrei.byfield@gmail.com`) on dev + staging tenant `759a83e8-...` (the active dev tenant). Note: `employees_email_unique_idx` is GLOBAL on `lower(email)` (not per-tenant), so a single email can only have one employees row across the entire system ŌĆö the second dev tenant `b62b764d-...` accesses Activities via the seeAll bypass (Dre's accounts are superadmin/manager there). **Test coverage** (`backend/__tests__/lib/resolveAssignedTo.test.js`, 11 cases on Node native test runner): UUID passthrough (with case-insensitivity), emailŌåÆemployees.id resolution with tenant + ilike normalization assertions, no-match returns null with NEGATIVE assertion that the users-table is NOT queried (regression guard), supabase error/throw graceful degrade, falsy / non-string / non-email-non-UUID input handling. **In progress towards 4VD-44.**

- **Signing activity hyperlink read "View Lead" instead of the actual entity name ŌĆö calling-convention bug on `resolveRelatedEntityFields` (4VD-43 day 4a regression) (`backend/lib/signingActivityTracker.js`, `backend/__tests__/lib/signingActivityTracker.test.js`)**: After the FK fix below landed and activities started persisting, the timeline rendered every signing activity's "Related To" hyperlink as the generic fallback "View Lead" / "View Contact" ŌĆö not the entity's actual display name. Live SQL audit on dev: 13/13 signing-source activity rows (12 backfilled + 1 from the live route post-deploy) had `related_name = NULL`. **Cause**: `resolveRelatedEntityFields` exports a positional signature `(supabase, tenantId, relatedTo, relatedId)`, used positionally everywhere else (calcom-webhook.js, activities.v2.js, workflowExecutionService.js, the helper's own test suite). `createSendActivity` was the lone caller passing a single object argument ŌĆö `{ supabase, tenantId, relatedTo: ..., relatedId: ... }`. JavaScript happily accepted that as the `supabase` positional, and the other three params became `undefined`. The helper's first guard line is `if (!supabase || !tenantId || !relatedTo || !relatedId) return empty;` ŌĆö it bailed silently and returned `{ related_name: null, related_email: null }` on every call. **Fix**: switched the call site to positional invocation: `resolveRelatedEntityFields(supabase, tenantId, session.related_to, session.related_id)`. Inline comment block explains the regression so future agents don't re-introduce the object-style call. **Test coverage extension** (4 new cases on the existing tracker test suite): (a) lead row with `first_name`+`last_name` composes into "Test Lead" on `related_name`; (b) account row with single `name` field maps to `related_name` directly; (c) missing entity row ŌåÆ both fields null, no throw, insert still proceeds; (d) the leads lookup filters on BOTH `tenant_id` AND `id` (cross-tenant defense ŌĆö pinned in case anyone tries to "simplify" the helper later). Fake supabase test harness extended with `leadRow` / `contactRow` / `accountRow` overrides so future tests can target any entity type. **No backfill required** ŌĆö Dre deleted the dev activity rows manually before the fix landed; new sends will populate `related_name` correctly from the start. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **Signing activity rows missing from Activities timeline ŌĆö silent FK violation on `assigned_to` (4VD-43 day 4a regression) (`backend/lib/signingActivityTracker.js`, `backend/routes/submissions.js`, `backend/__tests__/lib/signingActivityTracker.test.js`, dev DB backfill SQL)**: User reported zero signing-related rows showing up in the Activities timeline despite 20 sessions being created across both dev tenants today. Root cause: `createSendActivity` was passing `req.user.id` (a Supabase Auth users.id UUID) into `activities.assigned_to`, but that column has a FK to `employees(id)`, not `users(id)`. Every insert violated the FK and threw ŌĆö silently swallowed by the `.catch(() => undefined)` wrapper at the call site. Result: 0 of 20 sessions had matching activity rows. **Fix in tracker**: new `resolveAssignedEmployee(supabase, tenantId, userEmail)` helper looks up `employees.id` for the auth user's email scoped to the same tenant via `ilike` (case-insensitive), returns null when no match. `createSendActivity` signature changed: `assignedTo` (single arg, was being filled with users.id) ŌåÆ `sentByUserId` + `sentByUserEmail` (two args; user*id stashed in metadata for audit, email used for the employee lookup). When no employee row matches the email, `assigned_to` stays null ŌĆö no FK violation, row still inserts, audit metadata still captures the user identifiers. **Fix in submissions.js**: `POST /api/submissions` call site now passes `sentByUserEmail: req.user?.email` alongside `sentByUserId: req.user?.id`. **Backfill on dev branch (`nrtrjsatmsosslxwlmoj`)**: ran an INSERTŌĆ”SELECT joining `signing_sessions` to `signing_templates` to populate the 20 missing activity rows, mapping signing status ŌåÆ activity status (`pending`/`viewed` ŌåÆ pending, `signed`/`completed` ŌåÆ completed, `declined`/`expired` ŌåÆ cancelled), pre-stamping the lifecycle metadata slots (`viewed_at`/`signed_at`/`declined_at` from `updated_at` where appropriate), `assigned_to` left null for retroactive rows since auth-user attribution wasn't recorded. Verification post-backfill: 20/20 sessions have exactly one activity row each. Staging + prod don't have signing_sessions populated yet (dev-only feature still); no backfill needed there. **Test coverage** (`backend/__tests__/lib/signingActivityTracker.test.js`, 4 new cases on Node native test runner): (a) employees lookup returns a match ŌåÆ assigned_to populated with employees.id, sent_by_user*_ mirrored into metadata; (b) lookup misses ŌåÆ assigned*to null, no FK violation; (c) no email passed ŌåÆ lookup is skipped entirely (verified by absence of the employees-table call); (d) core metadata fields populated for downstream lifecycle-update path (signing_session_id, template_name, recipient*_, lifecycle slots pre-allocated as null, source tag = '4vd-43-signing'). **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

- **SignPage layout: bypass the global `body .mx-auto / .container / [class*='max-w-']` `!important` rule that was stretching the 720px PDF page-div to viewport width and pushing field overlays off-canvas (4VD-43 day 4b post-mortem) (`src/pages/SignPage.jsx`, `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx`)**: Multi-iteration debugging of "PDF on left, text inputs floating right" finally rooted in `src/styles/layout-theme.css` lines 48-59 ŌĆö a CRM-wide rule (`body [class*='max-w-'], body .mx-auto, body .container, main [class*='max-w-'], main .mx-auto, main .container, main .overflow-x-auto { max-width: 100% !important; width: 100% !important; margin-left: 0 !important; margin-right: 0 !important; }`). The rule is desirable for the CRM Layout (Activities-style full-width cards) but is loaded globally because CSS module imports in JS-land are still global. SignPage's PDF page-div used `mx-auto` for centering + inline `style={{ width: '720px' }}` for sizing ŌĆö the `!important` from the stylesheet beat the inline style, stretching the page-div to viewport. Field overlays positioned as percentages of the (now-stretched) parent landed far to the right of the 720px canvas, matching the user's screenshot exactly. Inline styles cannot beat `!important` from a stylesheet rule, so the only durable fix is to avoid the offending class names entirely: removed `mx-auto` from the page-div (replaced with inline `marginLeft: 'auto', marginRight: 'auto'`), removed `container mx-auto` from the header (replaced with inline `width: 100%, maxWidth: 1280px, margin: auto`), removed the `<main>`'s previously-used Tailwind classes in favor of fully inline `style={{ maxWidth: '768px', marginLeft: 'auto', marginRight: 'auto', padding: ... }}`. Page-div also retains its inline `width: ${p.widthPx}px` and `overflow-hidden` (latter is NOT matched by `[class*='overflow-x-auto']`, only the literal `overflow-x-auto` is, so it's safe). Documented the gotcha with an inline comment block at the top of `PageShell()` so future contributors don't accidentally re-introduce the offending classes. **Regression test**: `src/pages/__tests__/SignPage.smoke.test.jsx` parses `SignPage.jsx` source (after stripping comments to avoid matching the explanatory note) and asserts no `className="...mx-auto..."`, `...container...`, `...overflow-x-auto...`, or `...max-w-X...` on layout elements (`<div|main|header|section|article>`); also pins the inline-style replacements (`maxWidth: '768px'`, `marginLeft/marginRight: 'auto'`, `width: ${p.widthPx}px`, `RENDER_WIDTH_PX = 720`) and the field-overlay percentage math (`left: ${area.x * 100}%`, etc.). Lives in the `crm` vitest project (matches `src/pages/__tests__/*.smoke.test.{jsx,tsx}`). **Not addressed in this PR**: the broader CRM-wide stylesheet itself stays unchanged ŌĆö scoping `body [...]` to `body.app-shell [...]` would require adding the wrapper class to `Layout.jsx` AND audit-checking every other public page (AcceptInvite, AuthReset, ForgotPassword, FunnelDemo, the `/leads/:id`/`/accounts/:id`/`/contacts/:id` profile views) for the same class quirks; tracked separately, fix here is local to SignPage. **In progress towards 4VD-43.**

### Added

- **In-house eSign engine v1, day 1: schema + POST /api/templates + tests + UI rewire (4VD-43) (`backend/migrations/162_signing_templates.sql`, `backend/migrations/163_signing_sessions.sql`, `backend/routes/templates.js`, `backend/__tests__/routes/templates.test.js`, `backend/server.js` (route mount), `src/pages/DocumentTemplates.jsx` (list + builder repointed at /api/templates))**: First slice of the post-DocuSeal eSign engine. **Schema** ŌĆö two new tables on the dev preview branch (`nrtrjsatmsosslxwlmoj`) and staging (`bjedfowimuwbcnruwcdj`); deferred from prod until v1 ships. `public.signing_templates` (id, tenant*id FK, name, pdf_storage_path, fields jsonb, created/updated/archived timestamps) holds the per-tenant template catalogue: PDF lives in Supabase Storage at `tenant-assets/<tenant_id>/templates/<template_id>.pdf`, field placement in the `fields` jsonb (BuilderField[] schema from `src/lib/docusealFieldCoords.js`). `public.signing_sessions` (id, tenant_id, template_id FK, related_to/related_id polymorphic ref, recipient_email/name, signing_token UNIQUE, status enum, signed_pdf_storage_path, field_values jsonb, audit jsonb, message, expires_at default now()+14days, lifecycle timestamps) holds one row per recipient per send ŌĆö `signing_token` is the 32-byte hex capability the public `/sign/<token>` page will gate on, `audit` jsonb is the legal trail (IP+UA+timestamp per action). Both tables RLS-enabled with the standard 4-policy pattern (`tenant_id = current_tenant_id()` for SELECT/INSERT/UPDATE/DELETE, scoped to `authenticated`); service-role bypass remains available for the public signing route which authenticates on token presence rather than JWT. Naming chosen as `signing*\*`(not`templates`) to avoid collision with the existing generic `public.templates`table that backs`email_template`/`workflow_template`. **Backend route** ŌĆö `backend/routes/templates.js`exposes`POST /api/templates`, `GET /api/templates`, `GET /api/templates/:id`, `PUT /api/templates/:id`, `DELETE /api/templates/:id`. POST validates name (Ōēż200 chars, trimmed), base64 PDF (decoded to Buffer, 25MB ceiling, magic-byte sniff for `%PDF-`header), and the fields array (per-field name + type Ōłł {name,email,signature,date,text,checkbox} + duplicate-name detection + per-area page integer Ōēź0 + x/y/w/h Ōłł [0,1] + finite-number guards + non-empty areas array). PDF is uploaded to Supabase Storage FIRST; only after upload success does the row insert run, so a failed insert triggers a compensating storage-object delete (no orphan files, no orphan rows). Tenant isolation:`tenant_id = req.tenant.id`is stamped at the route layer;`external_id`-style client overrides are ignored. PUT validates name/fields the same way; PDF is immutable post-create (intentional ŌĆö protects existing `signing_sessions`that reference the template_id). DELETE is a soft delete via`archived_at`so signing sessions in flight don't break. **Server wiring** ŌĆö mounted at`/api/templates`in`backend/server.js`line 342 with`defaultLimiter + authenticateRequest`middleware (matches the`/api/storage`pattern). **Tests** ŌĆö`backend/**tests**/routes/templates.test.js`: 40 cases covering `validateSigningFields`(happy path, all 6 type variants, type rejection, empty/non-array/null input, empty-name/whitespace-name/duplicate-name, missing/empty areas, negative-coord/coord>1/non-integer-page/negative-page/NaN/Infinity rejection, default-required logic, default-role 'First Party'),`validateTemplateInput`(valid name + minimal PDF, name trim, empty-name/whitespace/over-200-chars rejection, empty-file/non-string-file rejection, non-PDF-magic-bytes rejection, 25MB ceiling), and`buildTemplateStorageKey`(tenant-scoped path, deterministic). **Frontend** ŌĆö`DocumentTemplates.jsx`rewired: list endpoint switched from`GET /api/docuseal/templates`to`GET /api/templates`, "+ New Template" button re-enabled, builder save points at `POST /api/templates`. The previous DocuSeal pivot's banner removed since the create flow is functional again. Note: existing DocuSeal admin-created templates no longer appear in this list (different table); the Send Document dialog still surfaces them via its own `GET /api/docuseal/templates`consumer until v1 fully ships and DocuSeal is decommissioned. **Reused unchanged**:`src/lib/docusealFieldCoords.js`(pure module, schema-agnostic ŌĆö pending rename to`signingFieldCoords.js`in a follow-up commit) and`src/components/docuseal/TemplateBuilderCanvas.jsx`(PDF render + drag/drop overlay UI). **Verification**: 40/40 backend tests pass via host node:test; ESLint clean (0 errors, 0 warnings) on both`backend/routes/templates.js`and`src/pages/DocumentTemplates.jsx`. **Out of scope for day 1** (next sessions per 4VD-43): `POST /api/submissions`(send-for-signing flow),`/sign/<token>` public renderer, pdf-lib stamping, audit trail wiring, Certificate of Completion appending, Playwright E2E.

### Removed

- **DocuSeal template-creation proxy + tests; UI builder mode disabled (4VD-28 pivot ŌĆö research correction) (`backend/routes/docuseal.js` POST `/templates` now returns 410 Gone, `buildCreateTemplateRequestBody` + `createDocusealTemplate` helpers deleted, `backend/__tests__/routes/docuseal-create-template.test.js` deleted, `src/pages/DocumentTemplates.jsx` reverted to list-only with disabled "+ New Template" button + banner explaining the rebuild, `scripts/inventory-out/esign-alternatives-2026-05-06.md` updated with ERRATUM block, Linear 4VD-28 re-scoped + child ticket 4VD-43 filed for the in-house engine build)**: Live probe against our self-hosted DocuSeal Community on 2026-05-09 returned `{"status":404,"message":"This feature is available in Pro Edition: https://www.docuseal.com/pricing"}` from `POST /api/templates/pdf` ŌĆö the endpoint the entire 4VD-28 plan was built around. The May 6 eSign-alternatives research had stated this endpoint was Community-free; that was inferred from upstream marketing pages, not from a probe, and was wrong. **Actual Community-free DocuSeal API surface**: `GET /api/templates*` (list/read) and `POST /api/submissions` (send-for-signing against an existing template) only. Template creation through any API endpoint is Pro-gated ŌĆö `/api/templates/pdf`, `/api/templates/docx`, `/api/templates/html`, and `<docuseal-builder>` web component all require a Pro license key on self-hosted Community. Same paywall that disqualified OpenSign in the original analysis, just behind different marketing. The ticket's plan ("build the field-placer in-house, POST to /api/templates/pdf") was structurally incomplete because the POST target doesn't exist on Community. **Pivot: build our own eSign engine** (option #4 from the path-forward analysis) ŌĆö drop DocuSeal as the upstream signing service entirely, replace with a CRM-native pipeline (templates table + Supabase Storage for PDFs + `/sign/<token>` renderer over `pdfjs-dist` + `pdf-lib` for signature stamping + audit trail + Certificate of Completion). 6ŌĆō8 dev days for v1, vs. ongoing Pro license cost or fragile DB-poking into DocuSeal's internals. **Rollback artifacts kept on disk for reuse in 4VD-43**: `src/lib/docusealFieldCoords.js` (pure module ŌĆö schema-agnostic 0ŌĆō1 normalized area math, will be renamed `signingFieldCoords.js`); `src/components/docuseal/TemplateBuilderCanvas.jsx` (PDF render + drag/drop overlay UI ŌĆö signing-engine-agnostic, will repoint at the new POST /api/templates endpoint). **Deprecation surfacing**: the now-disabled `POST /api/docuseal/templates` returns 410 Gone with a deprecation pointer rather than 404'ing through to DocuSeal, so any stale frontend client gets a clear migration message. **Customer impact**: zero ŌĆö the existing `Send Document` flow still works against templates created in DocuSeal admin (`GET /api/docuseal/templates` is Community-free); tenants who want new templates create them in DocuSeal admin until 4VD-43 ships, and they appear in the CRM list automatically. **Doppler `DOCUSEAL_PLATFORM_*` vars** staged into prd configs earlier this session can stay (env-only, no code reads them in prod, no harm; they'll be removed when DocuSeal infrastructure is fully retired). **Linear 4VD-43** ("In-house eSign engine v1") filed as a child of 4VD-28 with the full schema + endpoint + UI breakdown for the rebuild.

### Added

- **Schema-drift-safe integration test fixtures + dev-tenant re-homing ŌĆö `slug NOT NULL` constraint regression resolved (`.env`, Doppler `aishacrm/{dev,dev_personal}`, `backend/__tests__/testConstants.js`, `backend/__tests__/integration/userPermissions.integration.test.js`, `backend/__tests__/fixtures/dev-playground-seed.sql`, `backend/__tests__/ops/coolify-drift-guard.test.js`, dev-branch data-move on Supabase project `nrtrjsatmsosslxwlmoj`)**: `userPermissions.integration.test.js` was synthesizing a fresh tenant per run via `randomUUID()` and inserting `{id, tenant_id, name, status}` ŌĆö no `slug`. After the recent schema migration that added `slug NOT NULL` to `public.tenant`, every run produced 13 cascading `cancelledByParent` failures, and the failures **were** the schema drift detector working ŌĆö exactly what the integration tests are for. **Root cause clarified**: dev points at the preview branch `nrtrjsatmsosslxwlmoj` (parent staging), the seeded dev tenant is `759a83e8-...` ("Dev Local Tenant", `slug=dev-local-tenant`), and the seeded admin is `214086c9-...` (`abyfield@4vdataconsulting.com`) ŌĆö both established by `.warp/notebooks/supabase-dev-branch-reset.md ┬¦7` after Dre rebased staging off prod and branched dev off staging. **Fix**: (1) `.env` (root) gained `TEST_TENANT_ID=759a83e8-...` and `TEST_USER_ID=214086c9-...` with a comment pointing at the seed-source notebook; (2) Doppler `aishacrm/dev` and `aishacrm/dev_personal` got the same two values via `set_secrets` MCP so the Docker container picks them up via `doppler run`; (3) `testConstants.js` refreshed: `DEV_LOCAL_TENANT_ID = '759a83e8-...'` is the new canonical default for the `TENANT_ID` resolution chain (`process.env.TEST_TENANT_ID || STAGING_TENANT_ID || DEV_LOCAL_TENANT_ID`), `DEV_PLAYGROUND_TENANT_ID` aliased to it for back-compat with existing imports, new `TEST_USER_ID` export with `process.env.TEST_USER_ID` override; (4) `userPermissions.integration.test.js` no longer inserts a tenant ŌĆö `before()` verifies the seeded tenant exists (fail-loud if the dev branch has drifted from the seed; fix the seed, don't paper over here) and `after()` only deletes the test-owned teams/users/employees, never the seeded tenant; (5) `dev-playground-seed.sql` rewritten to seed the new tenant with `slug='dev-local-tenant'`, employees/teams/users all moved under `759a83e8-...` instead of the old playground UUID `b62b764d-...`. **Live data move on dev branch** (via `execute_sql` MCP): 6 employees (`aa000001-*`) and 2 teams (`bb000001-*`) and 1 legacy admin user (`04d1b289-...`) UPDATE'd from `tenant_id='b62b764d-...'` to `tenant_id='759a83e8-...'` so existing tests that import `EMP_*`/`TEAM_*` constants from `testConstants.js` continue to find their seeded fixtures under the new canonical tenant. Post-move counts on `759a83e8-`: 6 employees, 2 teams, 7 team_members, 2 users ŌĆö exactly matching the pre-move topology under playground. The old `b62b764d-` tenant row remains in place but is now childless (safe to GC later if needed). **Drift-guard test (4VD-37) skip in Docker**: `__tests__/ops/coolify-drift-guard.test.js` reads `scripts/install-coolify-drift-guard.ps1` whose source is excluded from the backend image by `backend/.dockerignore` lines 22ŌĆō26 (`scripts`, `*.ps1`, `*.sh`). Suite now wraps `node:test`'s `test` with a `{skip: SKIP_REASON}` flag when `existsSync(INSTALLER_PATH)` returns false; in Docker, all 12 cases skip cleanly with the reason printed; on host (where `scripts/` is present) they run as before. The drift guard's actual deploy target is `/usr/local/bin` on VPS-2, not the runtime backend, so the test was never appropriate for the Docker test surface. **Verification**: 114/114 docuseal regressions still green inside the rebuilt container; `node --check` clean on all touched test files. Pre-existing integration-test hang in `__tests__/ai/aiTriggersWorker.test.js` after `Suggestion Template Generation` is unrelated to this work ŌĆö separate concern (open Supabase HTTP handle blocking process exit).

- **CRM-native template builder UI ŌĆö end-user-testable wizard for placing fields on a PDF (4VD-28 v1 MVP) (`src/pages/DocumentTemplates.jsx`, `src/components/docuseal/TemplateBuilderCanvas.jsx`, `src/pages/index.jsx`, `src/utils/navigationConfig.js`, `src/pages/Layout.jsx`, `package.json` + `pdfjs-dist@4` and `react-rnd@10` added)**: New nav entry "Document Templates" (FileText icon) routes to `/DocumentTemplates`. List view enumerates existing templates from `GET /api/docuseal/templates`; "+ New Template" enters builder mode where the user uploads a PDF, picks fields from a sidebar (`name, email, signature, date, text, checkbox` ŌĆö the v1 scope frozen in `src/lib/docusealFieldCoords.js`), drags/resizes them via `react-rnd` over a `pdfjs-dist`-rendered canvas, then clicks **Save Template** to POST through the `external_id`-stamping proxy at `POST /api/docuseal/templates`. After save, the new template is immediately available in the existing **Send Document** dropdown on every contact / lead / account / opportunity panel ŌĆö closing the white-label loop end-to-end (no DocuSeal admin bounce). **AGPL ┬¦7(b) attribution** lives in the page footer ("Powered by DocuSeal" link to docuseal.com) ŌĆö do not remove. **Lazy-load**: `TemplateBuilderCanvas` is `React.lazy`-imported so the heavy `pdfjs-dist` + `react-rnd` chunk (~400KB gz) only loads when the builder is opened, keeping the entry chunk under 4VD-41's 600KB target. **PDF coords**: render-width pinned at 640 CSS px so DocuSeal's normalized 0-1 areas stay stable regardless of viewport; the worker file is loaded via Vite's `?url` import (`pdfjs-dist/build/pdf.worker.mjs?url`). **Tenant isolation**: client never passes `external_id` ŌĆö the backend proxy stamps `req.tenant.id` (4VD-15 invariant). **What's still NOT in this MVP** (next session): edit-existing-template flow, multi-page wizard niceties, `GET/PUT/DELETE /:id` proxy routes (only POST exists today), Playwright E2E for the uploadŌåÆplaceŌåÆsaveŌåÆlist round-trip. Linting clean (0 errors, 0 warnings on both new files). **In progress towards 4VD-28.**

- **CRM-native template builder foundation: pure coordinate-math module (FE) + POST /api/docuseal/templates proxy (BE) (4VD-28 ŌĆö partial; FE wizard still TODO) (`src/lib/docusealFieldCoords.js`, `src/lib/__tests__/docusealFieldCoords.test.js`, `backend/routes/docuseal.js` POST /templates handler + `buildCreateTemplateRequestBody` + `createDocusealTemplate` exports, `backend/__tests__/routes/docuseal-create-template.test.js`)**: First slice of the CRM-native template builder that closes the GoHighLevel-vs-us white-label gap by removing the per-tenant bounce out to `https://docuseal.aishacrm.com/templates`. **Pure FE module** ŌĆö `pixelToNormalized(box, pageDims)` converts pdfjs canvas pixel coords to DocuSeal's top-left-origin normalized 0-1 area shape; `normalizedToPixel(area, pageDims)` is the inverse used when loading an existing template back into the editor; `builderFieldToDocuseal(field, pageDimsByPage)` validates a single editor field and produces the wire entry; `buildDocusealFieldsPayload(fields, pageDimsByPage)` builds the full `fields` array with duplicate-name detection. No Y-flip needed (both browser and DocuSeal areas are top-left); 0.5px slack tolerated for react-rnd sub-pixel rounding; out-of-bounds, zero-size, NaN/Infinity, non-integer page numbers, and duplicate field names all throw with descriptive errors so a typo in the editor can't silently emit a malformed template. Field-type set frozen to v1 scope (`name`, `email`, `signature`, `date`, `text`, `checkbox`); signature defaults `required=true`, everything else `false`; default role `'First Party'`. Pure module ŌĆö no React, no DOM, no fetch. **Backend proxy route** `POST /api/docuseal/templates` accepts `{ name, documents: [{ name, file: base64 }], fields: [...] }`, validates via the new pure `buildCreateTemplateRequestBody({ name, externalId, documents, fields })` helper, ALWAYS stamps `external_id = req.tenant.id` (4VD-15 invariant ŌĆö never trusts a client-supplied external_id), then calls `createDocusealTemplate({ apiKey, baseUrl, body, fetchImpl })` which posts to upstream `POST /api/templates/pdf` with the platform `X-Auth-Token` header and unwraps both bare-object and `{data: ...}` response shapes. Cache invalidation: `templatesCache.delete(tenantId)` after a successful create so the next list/dropdown call sees the new template immediately. Error mapping: 4xx upstream ŌåÆ 4xx with `{error, status, body}` (truncated to 500 chars), 5xx ŌåÆ 503 `docuseal_unreachable`, malformed response ŌåÆ 502 `docuseal_response_invalid`, missing platform creds ŌåÆ 400 `docuseal_platform_not_configured` with operator-friendly message pointing at Doppler. **Tests** ŌĆö `docusealFieldCoords.test.js` (Vitest, frontend; ~22 cases): pixelŌåÆnormalized math (top-left, bottom-right, no Y-flip), zero-size/out-of-bounds/non-integer-page rejection, sub-pixel slack, NaN/Infinity rejection, normalizedToPixel inverse, round-trip preservation, builder-field validation (signature default-required, role default 'First Party', unsupported types rejected, empty names rejected, missing pageDims for a page rejected), payload building (multi-field order preserved, empty array rejected, duplicate names rejected, non-array rejected, non-Map pageDims rejected), FIELD_TYPES contract pin. `docuseal-create-template.test.js` (node:test, backend; 17 cases): canonical wire shape, name trim, document-N name fallback, externalId argument honored over any other source, empty/non-string externalId rejected, name validation (empty + >200 chars), empty documents/fields/non-array rejected, fetch wire format (URL, X-Auth-Token, Content-Type, Accept, JSON body), `{data: ...}` unwrap, 4xx error with status+body, 5xx error, network throw passthrough. **Full backend DocuSeal regression**: 114/114 pass across 7 test files (`docuseal-webhook`, `docuseal-events`, `docuseal-webhook-collapse`, `docuseal-external-id`, `docuseal-webhook-platform-secret`, `docuseal-create-template`, `docuseal-resolve-template-name`) ŌĆö was 86 before this slice. **What's NOT in this slice (still TODO under 4VD-28)**: the React `/templates/builder` route + `pdfjs-dist` lazy load + `react-rnd` field overlay UI; `GET /:id`, `PUT /:id`, `DELETE /:id` proxy routes; "Powered by DocuSeal" attribution footer; Playwright E2E covering uploadŌåÆplaceŌåÆsaveŌåÆlist. Foundation is solid and tenant isolation is pinned by tests so the UI work in the next session can call into stable wire-format primitives instead of inventing them. **In progress towards 4VD-28**.

- **DocuSeal Braid tool ŌĆö AiSHA can send documents in chat + fix two registry generator bugs that silently downgraded 10 tools to READ_ONLY (4VD-10) (`braid-llm-kit/examples/assistant/docuseal.braid`, `braid-llm-kit/tools/generate-registry.js`, `braid-llm-kit/tools/sync-registry.js`, `braid-llm-kit/tools/__tests__/registry-policy-inference.test.js`, `backend/lib/braid/registry.js`)**: New `.braid` file exposes three functions to AiSHA's tool-calling layer: `listDocusealTemplates`, `listDocusealSubmissions`, `sendDocumentForSigning`. Tenant isolation is already enforced server-side via `external_id=tenant_id` from 4VD-15, so the Braid wrappers just relay calls. With 4VD-34's template-name resolver also in place, the activity timeline now reads "Document sent ŌĆö NDA" end-to-end. **While running `npm run braid:sync` I noticed `sendDocumentForSigning` was registered as `policy: 'READ_ONLY'` despite the `.braid` declaring `@policy(WRITE_OPERATIONS)`.** Two real bugs surfaced in the registry generator: **(1) `inferPolicy()` ignored `@policy` annotations entirely** ŌĆö both `generate-registry.js` and `sync-registry.js` used a hardcoded name-prefix heuristic (`create`/`update`/`delete`/`mark`/...) and silently misclassified any function whose name didn't match. Fixed: read `fn.annotations[i]` where `i.name === 'policy'`, use declared value as source of truth, fall back to heuristic only when no annotation present (legacy files). Heuristic also expanded with `send`/`publish`/`archive`/`promote`. `DELETE_OPERATIONS` coerces to `WRITE_OPERATIONS` for the registry's two-bucket schema. Unknown policy strings reject (fall through to heuristic) so a typo can't emit invalid data. **(2) `compareRegistries()` only compared tool names, not values** ŌĆö `sync-registry.js` detected added/removed tools but NOT changed values. Even after fixing `inferPolicy`, it would have emitted "in sync" because the SET of tool names was identical.
